Later, we finally compromised and booked both rooms for one night at the hotel, and the lady from the reservation depar**ent was very helpful in arranging them next to each other. But this time at the Nuojin Resort Hotel, no matter which platform the reservation is made on, adjacent rooms are required to be arranged immediately and painfully. When checking in at the VIP building, it was clearly explained to the front desk that there were 2 rooms for 3 nights, and the deposit was fully paid for 2 rooms for 3 nights. It was the employees who explained later that repeatedly passed the responsibility for the hotel's work mistakes to the customer's ordering platform. My husband was passing by and asked the aunt to please open the door, but she didn't come to open the door. It wasn't until I called the switchboard for the second time that my aunt came over in a hurry. In short, during the whole stay, the service was not as comfortable as Nuojin. msg:Every rating is given very carefully, for fear that if it is not objective at all, it may mislead subsequent passengers. But this is a hotel that I would give 4 five stars without hesitation.
1. The location of the hotel is great. The top viewing platform is not open during the National Day, but we can still see the Forbidden City from our room. Ten minutes walk to Wangfujing.
2. Generally, old hotels have outdated decorations. Even if they are well maintained, the design is still a bit old-fashioned. But when the elevator opens on the floor, what comes into view is the milky white passage, which is simple and elegant. The entire design seems to be at the Venetian in Macau. It is a bright and energetic scent.
3. Closed hotels are usually a bit boring, and old-fashioned hotels can even feel very depressing. Surprisingly, there is a fresh air system in the room! The classical and elegant style of the room, coupled with the fresh air, infinitely adds to the comfort of the room.
4. The service attitude at the front desk needs to be improved! However, the attitude of the housekeeping staff is quite good! Fast response, high efficiency, and good quality work! The five stars for this service are purely for the proactive housekeeping staff.
5. Suggestion: In the hotel's parking lot, guests still have to pay a parking fee (60 yuan a day). This paid service is acceptable, but it is recommended that the parking lot be equipped with an extra security person to be responsible for guiding and assisting vehicles in and out of the parking lot. There is a huge flow of people on Chang'an Avenue, and they are constantly shuttling at the entrances and exits of vehicles. Many pedestrians even suddenly stop in front of walking vehicles to take pictures of the hotel's facade, which is very dangerous. Getting in and out of the parking lot requires endless patience and patience. luck. The policeman on guard at the intersection of the hotel suggested moving in directly, but this required the cooperation of pedestrians. I would also like to give some advice to future travelers, not to rush in for the moment. Because of such a troublesome way to get in and out, our car was parked directly in the hotel parking lot for several days without moving. We had to take a taxi to get in and out. If an additional conductor can be added, the safety of all parties will be respected and guaranteed.
